add_namespace = ksr

#Transfer Transnistria (Offerer Side)
country_event = {
	id = ksr.1
	title = ksr.1.t
	desc = ksr.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #to Romania
		name = ksr.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_moldova_transnistria_state = yes
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						controller = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
				}
				ROM = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.4
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep it
		name = ksr.1.b
	}	
}



#Transfer Vladivostok-Khabarovsk (Offerer Side)

		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 408
						state = 1332
						state = 1333
						state = 1334
						state = 1335
						state = 1336
						state = 409
					}
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						controller = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
				}
				JAP = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.17
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep it
		name = ksr.2.b
	}	
}

# Transfer Transnistria (Receiver Side)
country_event = {

	id = ksr.4
	title = ksr.4.t
	desc = ksr.4.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ksr.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				KSR_is_moldova_transnistria_state = yes
				OR = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
					AND = {
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
						CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = ksr.21
					hours = 2
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = ksr.4.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.5
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}	
}

#Transfer Karelia (Offerer Side)
country_event = {
	id = ksr.6
	title = ksr.6.t
	desc = ksr.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #to Finland
		name = ksr.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_karelia_kola_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = FIN }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				FIN = { set_state_controller = PREV }
			}
		}
		FIN = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.7
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep it
		name = ksr.6.b
	}	
}

# Germany Claims Southern Jutland (Denmark)
country_event = {
	id = ksr.13
	title = ksr.13.t
	desc = ksr.13.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Accept demands
		name = ksr.13.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = GER
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
				GER = {
					surrender_progress > 0.09
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GER
					}
					DEN = {
						is_puppet_of = PREV
					}
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = ksr.14 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Refuse
		name = ksr.13.b		
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					GER = {
						surrender_progress > 0.09
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {
						NOT = {
							tag = GER
						}
						DEN = {
							is_puppet_of = PREV
						}
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					DEN = {
						is_puppet_of = GER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = DEN
				generator = { 934 }
				}
				country_event = { days = 1 id = ksr.15 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = ksr.15 }
			}
		}		
	}
}

	id = ksr.17
	title = ksr.17.t
	desc = ksr.17.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ksr.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 408
					state = 1332
					state = 1333
					state = 1334
					state = 1335
					state = 1336
					state = 409
				}
				OR = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
					AND = {
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
						CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = ksr.21
					hours = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ksr.17.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.18
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}	
}

# MAN IN THE HIGH CASTLE: Player gains event suggesting to send an offer to Germany/Japan to split-claim American territory
country_event = {
	id = ksr.22
	title = ksr.22.t
	desc = {
		text = ksr.22.GER.desc
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ksr.22.JAP.desc
		trigger = { tag = JAP }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_north_american_division_plan
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_initiated
	}
	

	option = {
		name = ksr.22.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
				}
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.23
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}


# MAN IN THE HIGH CASTLE: The other country receives the offer for the North American partition plan
country_event = {
	id = ksr.23
	title = ksr.23.t
	desc = ksr.23.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_north_american_division_plan
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.23.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = GER.ksr_nadp_states_array
			add_claim_by = GER
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = JAP.ksr_nadp_states_array
			add_claim_by = JAP
		}

		
		hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_signed }
		
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.24
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.23.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.25
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
	
}

#Transfer Sobrance: Offerer Side
country_event = {
	id = ksr.26
	title = ksr.26.t
	desc = ksr.26.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #to Hungary
		name = ksr.26.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					1148 = {
						OR = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							controller = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
				HUN = { set_state_controller = 1148 }
			}
		}
		HUN = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.27
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep it
		name = ksr.26.b
	}	
}

		}

			limit = {

					OR = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
						AND = {
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
							CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = FROM NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = 1148 }
		}
		
		
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {

					id = ksr.21
					hours = 2
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = ksr.27.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {

		name = ksr.30.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
				
					# Korean Peninsula + Jeju Island
					controls_state = 525
					controls_state = 527
					controls_state = 1311
					controls_state = 1031
					controls_state = 1313
					controls_state = 1030
					controls_state = 1315
					controls_state = 1316
					controls_state = 1317
					controls_state = 1318
					controls_state = 1029
					controls_state = 1320
					controls_state = 1321
					controls_state = 1322
					controls_state = 1323
					controls_state = 1324
					controls_state = 1028
					controls_state = 1326
					controls_state = 1327
					controls_state = 1328
					controls_state = 1329
				}
				
				has_war_with = JAP 
				has_capitulated = no
				
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = SOV
							is_subject_of = SOV
						}
						has_government = communism
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = PRC
							is_subject_of = PRC
						}
						has_government = communism
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							is_subject_of = CHI
						}
						is_ally_with = PRC
						PRC = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_subject = no
						NOT = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan }
					}
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = { NOT = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan } }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = yes }
				OVERLORD = { country_event = { id = ksr.31 days = 1 } }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = ksr.31 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.30.b
	}

}

# Korean Division Plan - USA POV - Prompt to Transfer Territory North of the 38th Parallel
country_event = {
	id = ksr.34
	title = ksr.34.t
	desc = ksr.34.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_korean_division_plan

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.34.a
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan } }
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					target = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = ksr.36 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan } }
			PRC = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					target = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = ksr.36 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.34.b
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 527
					state = 1320
					state = 1321
					state = 1322
					state = 1323
					state = 1324
					state = 1028
					state = 1326
					state = 1327
					state = 1328
					state = 1329
				}
				any_country = {
					owns_state = PREV
					controls_state = PREV
					OR = {
						tag = USA
						is_subject_of = USA
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan } }
				transfer_state_to = SOV
				hidden_effect = {
					SOV = { country_event = { id = ksr.35 hours = 2 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { PRC = { has_country_flag = KSR_accepted_korean_division_plan } }
				transfer_state_to = PRC
				hidden_effect = {
					PRC = { country_event = { id = ksr.35 hours = 2 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_full_control_of_state = 611
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1476
					has_full_control_of_state = 1476
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 612
					has_full_control_of_state = 612
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1441
					has_full_control_of_state = 1441
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1455
					has_full_control_of_state = 1455
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1456
					has_full_control_of_state = 1456
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1458
					has_full_control_of_state = 1458
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1459
					has_full_control_of_state = 1459
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1474
					has_full_control_of_state = 1474
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1475
					has_full_control_of_state = 1475
				}
				AND = {
					owns_state = 1043
					has_full_control_of_state = 1043
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ksr.45.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 611
					state = 1476
					state = 612
					state = 1441
					state = 1455
					state = 1456
					state = 1458
					state = 1459
					state = 1474
					state = 1475
					state = 1043
				}
				is_owned_by = JAP
				is_fully_controlled_by = JAP
			}
			MEN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			add_core_of = MEN
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			MEN = { set_cosmetic_tag = MEN_mongol_military_government }
			JAP = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						not = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = MEN
						autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						not = {
							has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = MEN
						autonomous_state = autonomy_puppet
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = MEN
						autonomous_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.45.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		trigger = {
			MAN = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
				has_capitulated = no
				
				any_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 611
						state = 1476
						state = 612
						state = 1441
						state = 1455
						state = 1456
						state = 1458
						state = 1459
						state = 1474
						state = 1475
						state = 1043
					}
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_owned_by = MAN
						is_fully_controlled_by = MAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 611
					state = 1476
					state = 612
					state = 1441
					state = 1455
					state = 1456
					state = 1458
					state = 1459
					state = 1474
					state = 1475
					state = 1043
				}
				is_owned_by = JAP
				is_fully_controlled_by = JAP
			}
			MAN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			add_core_of = MAN
		}
		
		MAN = {
			country_event = {
				id = ksr.46
				hours = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.45.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
}

# Protectorate of Bohemia-Moravia
country_event = {
	id = ksr.47
	title = ksr.47.t
	desc = ksr.47.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.47.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RKH = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = DISABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rp_bohmen_mahren_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKH }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKH = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rp_bohmen_mahren_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKH }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKH = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RKH = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 9
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 50000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 2 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = wuw_GER_reichskommissariats.13
			hours = 2
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RKH }
			set_autonomy = { target = RKH autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.47.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.48 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.47.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.49 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.47.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = RKH
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.47.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

# Reichskommissariat Niederlande - Manage Territories
country_event = {
	id = ksr.54
	title = ksr.54.t
	desc = ksr.54.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.54.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		trigger = {
			any_state = {
				KSR_is_rk_niederlande_state = yes
				NOT = { is_owned_by = RKN }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
							option = DISABLED
						}
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = { tag = RKN }
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
								option = ENABLED
							}
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
								option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
							}
						}
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = { tag = RKN }
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = DISABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_niederlande_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKN }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKN = {
					transfer_state = PREV 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_niederlande_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKN }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKN = {
					transfer_state = PREV 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.54.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.53 }
	}
}

# Reichskommissariat Belgien-Nordfrankreich
country_event = {
	id = ksr.56
	title = ksr.56.t
	desc = ksr.56.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.56.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RKB = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = DISABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_belgien_nordfrankreich_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKB }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_belgien_nordfrankreich_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKB }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKB = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RKB = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 6
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 50000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RKB }
			set_autonomy = { target = RKB autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = wuw_GER_reichskommissariats.1
			hours = 2
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.56.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKB = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.57 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.56.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKB = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.58 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.56.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKB = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = RKB
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.56.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

# Militarverwaltung Frankreich
country_event = {
	id = ksr.62
	title = ksr.62.t
	desc = ksr.62.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.62.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			MWF = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = DISABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_militarverwaltung_frankreich_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = MWF }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				MWF = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_militarverwaltung_frankreich_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = MWF }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				MWF = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			MWF = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 16
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = MWF }
			set_autonomy = { target = MWF autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.62.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			MWF = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.63 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.62.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			MWF = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.64 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.62.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			MWF = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = MWF
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.62.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.65.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RKO = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = DISABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_ostland_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKO }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = WW2_HISTORICAL_ONLY
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_ostland_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKO }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RKO = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 808
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 50000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = wuw_GER_reichskommissariats.5
			hours = 2
		}	
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RKO }
			set_autonomy = { target = RKO autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.65.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKO = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.66 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.65.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKO = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.67 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.65.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKO = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = RKO
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}

# Reichskommissariat Don-Wolga
country_event = {
	id = ksr.77
	title = ksr.77.t
	desc = ksr.77.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.77.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RDW = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_don_wolga_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RDW }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RDW = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_don_wolga_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RDW }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RDW = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RDW = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 218
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 50000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RDW }
			set_autonomy = { target = RDW autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.77.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RDW = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.78 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.77.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RDW = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.79 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.77.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RDW = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = RDW
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.77.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ksr.80
	title = ksr.80.t
	desc = ksr.80.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RKM = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_moskowien_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKM }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_moskowien_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RKM }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RKM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RKM = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 219
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 80000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 10000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 1000
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RKM }
			set_autonomy = { target = RKM autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
		
		country_event = {
			id = wuw_GER_reichskommissariats.8
			hours = 2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKM = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.81 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.80.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKM = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.82 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.80.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RKM = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}

# Order State of Burgundy
country_event = {
	id = ksr.98
	title = ksr.98.t
	desc = ksr.98.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.98.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			BRG = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_order_state_burgundy_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = BRG }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT

				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {

					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = BRG }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				BRG = {
					transfer_state = PREV 
					hidden_effect = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
							days = 365
						}
						set_capital = {
							state = 1257
							remember_old_capital = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			set_autonomy = { target = BRG autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate }
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = ksr.101
	title = ksr.101.t
	desc = ksr.101.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.101.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			ARH = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = ARH.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ARH
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					ARH = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = ARH.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ARH
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					ARH = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			ARH = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owns_state = 358 }
					set_capital = {
						state = 358
						remember_old_capital = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = ARH }
			set_autonomy = { target = ARH autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.101.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			ARH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.102 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.101.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			ARH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.103 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.101.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			ARH = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = ARH
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ksr.105.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
							option = ENABLED
						}
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = CRH.ksr_states_array
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = CRH
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
					any_of_scopes = {
						array = CRH.ksr_states_array
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = CRH
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = CRH.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = CRH

							OR = {
								tag = ROOT

							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}

				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = CRH.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = CRH
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					CRH = { transfer_state = PREV }

			}

	}

		}

				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JPS.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = JPS
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					JPS = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JPS.ksr_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							NOT = {
								tag = JPS
							}
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					JPS = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			JPS = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owns_state = 1167 }
					set_capital = {
						state = 1167
						remember_old_capital = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = JPS }
			set_autonomy = { target = JPS autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.107.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			JPS = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.108 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.107.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			JPS = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}

	}

			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {

# MAN IN THE HIGH CASTLE: One of the parties is informed that they own and control territory belonging to the other
country_event = {
	id = ksr.110
	title = ksr.110.t
	desc = ksr.110.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_north_american_division_plan
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_signed
		NOT = { has_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_broken }
		
		OR = {
			tag = GER
			tag = JAP
		}
		
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = GER
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = JAP.ksr_nadp_states_array
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						owns_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = JAP
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = GER.ksr_nadp_states_array
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						owns_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = ANZ.ksr_states_array
				CONTROLLER = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ksr.110.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}		
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.ksr_nadp_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					JAP = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				JAP = {
					country_event = {
						id = ksr.112
						hours = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}		
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = GER.ksr_nadp_states_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							OR = {
								tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = PREV
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					GER = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = ksr.112
						hours = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = ANZ.ksr_states_array
			if = {
				limit = {
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				ANZ = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.110.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = KSR_north_american_division_plan_war_threat_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = ksr.111
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ksr.111
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_signed
			set_global_flag = KSR_north_america_partition_broken
		}
	}
}




# MAN IN THE HIGH CASTLE: One of the parties is informed that they own and control territory belonging to the other
country_event = {
	id = ksr.111
	title = ksr.111.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_north_american_division_plan
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = ksr.111.GER.desc
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ksr.111.JAP.desc
		trigger = { tag = JAP }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.111.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = JAP
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					JPS = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = JPS
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = GER
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ARH = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = GER
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = ARH
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CRH = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject_of = GER
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = CRH
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ANZ
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = ANZ
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.111.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_north_american_division_plan

# Reichskommissariat Skandinavien
country_event = {
	id = ksr.113
	title = ksr.113.t
	desc = ksr.113.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_gerbrandy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.113.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			RSK = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		
		GER_improve_rosenbergs_trait_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
						option = ENABLED
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_skandinavien_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RSK }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						owns_state = PREV
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RSK = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = allow_ksr_subjects_on_controlled
					option = ENABLED
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					KSR_is_rk_skandinavien_state = yes
					CONTROLLER = {
						NOT = { tag = RSK }
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				RSK = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RSK = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown
					days = 365
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 141
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				add_manpower = 50000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}	
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = GER
				}	
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
				load_oob = "RK_OOB"
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			hidden_effect = { puppet = RSK }
			set_autonomy = { target = RSK autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.113.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RSK = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.114 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.113.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RSK = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = ksr.115 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.113.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			RSK = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				NOT = { has_idea = ksr_subject_creation_cooldown }
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = RSK
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ksr.113.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

# CHI annexes Warlord (puppet option for player)
country_event = {
	id = ksr.142
	title = ksr.142.t
	desc = ksr.142.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = ksr.142.a
		FROM = { annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}

	#Nothing
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		FROM = { puppet = ROOT }
		name = ksr.142.b
	}
}



# China receives prompt to annex collapsing Shandong Clique (circumstantial trigger)
country_event = {
	id = ksr.143
	title = ksr.143.t
	desc = ksr.143.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_infiltration
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = CHI
				has_war_with = JAP
				
				SND = {
					exists = yes
					has_war_with = JAP 
					has_capitulated = no
					surrender_progress > 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ksr.143.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SND = { country_event = { id = ksr.142 days = 1 } }
	}

	#Nothing
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = ksr.143.b
	}
}
